<section type="letter to the reader" lang="la"><term lang="la">
<heading>
&#182; Ad lectorum epistola.
</heading>

CVm de latinis vocabulis ex t<expan type="">em</expan>porale opuscu&#173;
lum n<expan type="">ostr</expan>o nomine (cl<expan type="">am</expan>me tam<expan type="">en</expan>) edit<expan type="">um</expan>:ac multa
istiuc ad<expan type="">em</expan>pta mutataq<expan type="">que</expan> vider<expan type="">em</expan> (vt <expan type="">quam</expan>uis cursim reco&#173;
gnit<expan type="">um</expan>) vt homini negocioso (licuit) n<expan type="">un</expan>c cultius et po&#173;
stulo apparatu prodiret: Cui vt magiscula habeatur
fideles: legis hic nichil candide lector quod non sit di<emend err="">&#173;</emend>
ctum prius. Caput prim<expan type="">um</expan>(quod de corporis anatho&#173;
mia inscribitur.) Ad verb<expan type="">um</expan> fere et primo de a<expan type="">anim</expan>alibus
(interprete / theodore) sumpt<expan type="">um</expan> est. Que vero de pisci<emend err="">&#173;</emend>
bus auibus herbisq<expan type="">que</expan> tradidi apud plint<expan type="">um</expan> leges alia:
alia vero in his quor<expan type="4">rum</expan> censure merrio st<expan type="">an</expan>d<expan type="">um</expan> duxeris.
Agricolationis arma &#38; id gen<expan type="">us</expan> (euoluto cathene ver<emend err="">&#173;</emend>
rone ac columella) in pr<expan type="">om</expan>ptu er<expan type="">un</expan>t. Reliqui pleraq<expan type="">que</expan> et
peroti cornicopie et alijs no<expan type="">is</expan>atissimis passim collegi
operib<expan type="">us</expan>. vbi (si qua in sint vicia) quisquis publice vti<emend err="">&#173;</emend>
litatis gratia potius <expan type="">quam </expan> curiositate adduct<expan type="">us</expan> ead<expan type="">en</expan>pse&#173;
rit (id <expan type="">quod</expan> cupidisissime fact<expan type="">um</expan> vell<expan type="">em</expan> offendet me nichil.
Elicubrar<expan type="">am</expan> hoc tenue opus n<expan type="">ostr</expan>is t<expan type="">amen</expan> discipulis verna
cul<expan type="">um</expan>: sed librario<expan type="4">rum</expan> temeritas n<expan type="">un</expan>c c<expan type="">omon</expan>e fecit ne<expan type="">que</expan> <expan type="">pro</expan>pte<emend err="">&#173;</emend>
rea volui priuat<expan type="">um</expan> <expan type="">quam</expan> alijs fruct<expan type="">um</expan> (si <expan type="">qui</expan>s inest) viderim:
immo <expan type="">quod</expan> nulla res potest esse ead<expan type="">em</expan> simul festinata et
examinata. Suadet horatius eiusmodi in nou<expan type="">um</expan> pre<emend err="">&#173;</emend>
mi animum Cui opt<expan type="">em</expan>perassem: nisi (velim nolim) ab 
officina i<expan type="">am</expan> extorquere<expan type="">tur</expan>: virgilian<expan type="">um</expan> adagi<expan type="">um</expan> est n<expan type="">on</expan> a<expan type="">nim</expan>a
possumus o<expan type="">mn</expan>es. Quocirca pro dictis horatij offendant
pauce macule nemin<expan type="">em</expan>. Alt<expan type="">que</expan> t<expan type="">am</expan> rem vbi contingit c<expan type="">om</expan>&#173;
moda vocatio pluscula (hauspice deo) accedens hec
versiculis sic (<expan type="">quam</expan>uis non obseruata lege) complexus 
sum: vt nimis hereat rudis inuentus. Vale
</term></section>
